### [233] [What Makes a Representational Prior Work? Feature Families, Label-Free Invariances, and Critical Windows in Grokking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12735)
*Gunner Levi Howe*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了对比先验在grokking现象中加速泛化的机制，通过188次实验验证了先验的作用依赖于特征族对齐、无标签不变性先验的有效性、早期施加窗口的关键性，以及结构化注入可大幅降低权重范数延迟律的指数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解grokking延迟的本质——即任务结构化表征形成所需的时间——并验证"先验通过作用于电路特征层面来影响泛化"这一核心预测。

Method: 在188组新实验下，沿四个轴（特征族对齐、监督方式、施加时机、实验设置）系统对比不同先验的效果，包括随机划分基线、无标签交换不变性先验、权重范数钳制等组合方案。

Result: 1) 错误特征族的先验阻碍泛化（与随机划分无显著差异，p=0.43）；2) 纯无标签交换不变性先验在15/15次运行中实现泛化，中位加速2.7倍，优于标签监督先验（p=0.038）；3) 早期窗口（前2000轮，占预算4%）即可实现10/10泛化，中位加速2.7倍，优于持续施加（8/10，1.25倍）；4) 结构注入使权重范数延迟律指数降低约17倍。

Conclusion: 特征族对齐决定先验是否允许泛化；无标签的不变性内容足以实现加速；早期短窗口即可捕获绝大部分收益。

Abstract: Companion work showed the grokking delay is causally the time to form task-structured representations, injectable via a contrastive prior. Here we characterize what makes such a prior work, across four axes, in 188 new runs. Content: a coherent, learnable prior built from the wrong feature family (magnitude bands) blocks generalization like a random partition (1/15 vs 0/20 grok; $p=0.43$ between them), confirming the companion's prediction that priors act at the level of the circuit's features. Supervision: a fully label-free invariance prior -- positives are commuted pairs $(a,b)\sim(b,a)$ only -- generalizes in 15/15 runs at a median $2.7\times$ speedup, more reliably than the label-supervised prior itself ($p=0.038$), and combined with a weight-norm clamp yields the strongest method we test (median $17\times$, 5/5) -- strongest meaning reliably fast: plain cross-entropy with a clamp matches this speed only at the exact critical norm, while the prior keeps it fast across the entire clamp range. Timing: the prior is only needed early -- applied solely during the first 2000 epochs (4% of budget) it generalizes 10/10 at $2.7\times$, beating continuous application (8/10, $1.25\times$) and a duration-matched later window ($2.1\times$). Setting: the dissociation replicates on modular multiplication and across depths and normalization variants, and a clamp sweep quantifies the companion's central claim: structure injection flattens the weight-norm delay-law exponent about 17-fold (plain cross-entropy slows $31\times$ per +10 norm units, a lower bound as higher cells are censored, versus $1.22\times$ with the prior). Honest boundary: tasks that generalize before memorizing have no delay to control. Feature-family alignment decides whether a prior permits generalization; invariance content suffices for acceleration without labels; a brief early window captures nearly all of the benefit.

### [234] [Constraint-Aware Aggregation for Federated Reinforcement Learning in Microgrid Energy Coordination](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12763)
*Usman Haider,Karl Mason*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种约束感知的联邦强化学习聚合方法，通过惩罚项加权聚合（权重与奖励减去违规惩罚成正比），在分布式能源协调任务中显著提升安全性（减少违规）并保持奖励水平，无需修改本地训练或进行对偶优化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准联邦强化学习方法（如FedAvg）在聚合时未考虑系统级约束，导致全局行为不安全。现有方法需要复杂的对偶优化或修改本地训练，缺乏轻量级解决方案。

Method: 提出约束感知的聚合规则：权重 $w_i \propto R_i - αV_i$（奖励减去违规惩罚），在服务端聚合时同时考虑本地性能与估计的约束违规，无需修改本地训练或进行对偶优化。

Result: 在DairyGridEnv基准（多农场电池储能协同）和真实负载数据（芬兰、德国FIELD数据集）上，惩罚加权聚合相比FedAvg显著减少违规，同时提升奖励。奖励-违规联合方案可调节但稳定性较差。

Conclusion: 轻量级聚合策略能够在保持标准通信协议的前提下，显著提高联邦强化学习的实际安全性。

Abstract: Federated Reinforcement Learning (FedRL) enables coordination of distributed energy resources without sharing raw local data, but standard aggregation methods such as FedAvg do not account for system-level constraints, often leading to unsafe global behavior. In this work, we study constraint-aware aggregation for federated reinforcement learning in distributed energy coordination. We propose aggregation rules that incorporate both local performance and estimated constraint violation into the server-side update. Among these, a simple penalty-based rule, $w_i \propto R_i - αV_i$, consistently provides the most reliable trade-off between reward and safety, without requiring dual optimization or modifications to local training. \textcolor{black}{We evaluate our approach on DairyGridEnv, a benchmark modeling multiple farms coordinating battery storage under stochastic demand and a shared grid capacity constraint, and further assess robustness using real load-driven demand profiles from Finland and the German FIELD dataset. Across multiple seeds, penalty-based aggregation substantially reduces violations while improving reward relative to FedAvg in both synthetic and real load-driven settings.} A combined reward-violation scheme exposes a tunable trade-off via $λ$, but is less stable. These results demonstrate that lightweight aggregation strategies can substantially improve empirical safety in federated reinforcement learning while preserving standard communication protocols.

### [235] [AVQ-Attention: Adaptive Vector-Quantized Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12789)
*Winfried van den dool,Patrick Forré,Amir Habibian,Yuki M. Asano,Max Welling*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出自适应向量量化注意力（AVQ Attention），通过动态分配码本容量来优先精细量化高注意力区域，在保持O(MN)复杂度下提升精度-效率权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准注意力机制O(N²)复杂度是计算瓶颈；VQ注意力虽降至O(MN)但码本容量均匀分配，导致高注意力区域被粗量化而低注意力区域浪费容量。

Method: 从少量码字开始，前向传播中识别最重要的码字，用预训练的子码字对其进行细化，实现高注意力区域精细量化、低注意力区域粗量化；基于自定义Triton内核在Flash Attention的平铺计算范式内完成整个过程。

Result: 在保持O(MN)复杂度的同时，相比固定码本的VQ注意力取得了更好的精度-效率权衡。

Conclusion: 自适应码本分配策略能有效解决VQ注意力中码本容量分配不均的问题，在不增加复杂度的情况下提升模型性能。

Abstract: The $\mathcal{O}(N^2)$ complexity of attention over $N$ tokens remains a computational bottleneck in transformer models. Vector-Quantized (VQ) attention reduces this to $\mathcal{O}(MN)$ by representing keys with $M$ codewords, but applies uniform codebook capacity regardless of where attention mass concentrates: high-attention regions of key space may be coarsely approximated while low-attention regions waste representational capacity. We propose Adaptive Vector-Quantized (AVQ) Attention, which adaptively allocates codebook capacity based on attention importance. Starting from a small set of codewords, our method identifies the most important codes during the forward pass and refines them with pre-learned child codewords, achieving fine-grained quantization where it matters most while maintaining coarse quantization elsewhere. We develop an implementation using custom Triton kernels that enables the full adaptive refinement process, including importance scoring, child codeword insertion, and parent contribution replacement, to be carried out within the tiled computation paradigm of Flash Attention with minimal overhead. Our approach maintains $\mathcal{O}(MN)$ complexity while achieving improved accuracy-efficiency trade-offs compared to fixed-codebook VQ-attention.

### [236] [Verifier-Based Reinforcement Fine-Tuning of Reasoning Models for Thermal Energy Storage Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12856)
*Takumi Shioda,Kohei Terashima,Tatsuo Nagai*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究利用强化学习与可验证奖励（RLVR），基于离线动态规划的动作价值，对开源推理模型进行微调，使其能够为建筑热储能系统制定日前调度策略。仅用30条训练提示，模型碳排放从70.5降至61.2 kg-CO2，接近动态规划最优值60.8 kg-CO2，且推理能力（而非单纯语言模型能力）对性能提升至关重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建筑需根据电网状态灵活调节冷负荷，热储能（TES）虽能实现负荷转移，但其调度需提前数小时规划并受存储约束。现有方法（MPC、强化学习）难以规模化推广至多栋建筑，因此需要一种可扩展且高效的调度方法。

Method: 将离线动态规划（DP）的精确动作价值转化为稠密奖励信号，通过强化学习与可验证奖励（RLVR）对开源推理模型进行微调（RFT）。模型作为上层调度器，基于文本状态和预测输出逐时热泵设定点。仅使用30条训练提示，在简单的办公建筑TES基准上验证。

Result: RFT将碳排放从70.5降至61.2 kg-CO2，接近DP最优值60.8 kg-CO2。GPT-5（推理模型）几乎匹配DP和MPC，而GPT-4o（非推理LLM）碳排放高于无储能基线。RFT主要稳定了候选比较、前瞻和可行性检查等规划模式，而非创造新策略。在预测误差和未见过的TES条件下，规划模式保持鲁棒，并泛化至电池任务但增益有限。

Conclusion: 基于DP的可验证奖励为适应开源推理模型到建筑储能调度提供了一种实用途径，结果激励在高保真度场景下进行全建筑控制测试，并开发城市级能源管理的可扩展验证器。

Abstract: Buildings are expected to shift cooling loads in response to grid conditions. Thermal energy storage (TES) enables this shift, but scheduling it well requires planning hours ahead under storage constraints. Model predictive control (MPC) and reinforcement learning are difficult to scale across buildings. This study instead adapts an open-weight reasoning model through reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR). We convert exact offline dynamic-programming (DP) action values into dense rewards for every candidate action. Using only 30 training prompts, reinforcement fine-tuning (RFT) trains the model as an upper-level scheduler that outputs hourly heat-pump setpoints from text-based states and forecasts. Evaluation uses a deliberately simple office-building TES benchmark where exact DP is tractable and the optimum is known. RFT reduces the open-weight model's emissions from 70.5 to 61.2 kg-CO2, close to the DP optimum of 60.8 kg-CO2. GPT-5 nearly matches DP and MPC without task-specific training, while GPT-4o, a non-reasoning LLM, produces higher emissions than the no-storage baseline, so inference-time reasoning appears important. Trace analysis shows that RFT mainly stabilizes observable planning patterns (candidate comparison, look-ahead, and feasibility checking) rather than creating a new strategy. Robustness and generalization tests clarify what transfers: the reinforced planning patterns persist under forecast errors and an unseen TES condition and carry over to a battery task, but its different structure limits the gains. DP-based verifiable rewards offer a practical way to adapt open-weight reasoning models to building storage scheduling. These results motivate higher-fidelity tests of whole-building control and scalable verifiers for city-scale energy management.

</details>


### [237] [Energy-Based Physics-Informed Form Finding for Clustered Tensegrity Structures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12888)
*Jing Qin,Muhao Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于能量的学习框架，用于解决张拉整体结构的找形和物理属性预测问题。该框架将总势能最小化和本构关系融入训练目标，能够同时预测平衡节点构型及杆件力、力密度等物理量，在棱柱和着陆器系统等数值实验中展现出良好的可扩展性和预测精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 张拉整体结构的找形和物理属性预测是力学中的基本逆问题，由于几何与力之间的强非线性耦合、结构稳定性要求以及边界条件、对称性等约束的存在，传统方法难以有效求解，且对噪声和异常值缺乏鲁棒性。

Method: 提出基于能量的学习框架，将总势能最小化和本构关系作为物理损失直接融入训练目标中，使模型能够同时学习平衡节点构型以及杆件力和力密度等物理量，提升物理一致性、鲁棒性和数据效率。

Result: 在张拉整体棱柱和着陆器系统上的数值实验表明，该方法在可扩展的找形和结构属性准确预测方面具有巨大潜力。

Conclusion: 基于能量的学习框架有效解决了张拉整体结构找形中的非线性和约束问题，相比传统方法具有更好的鲁棒性和物理一致性，为集群张拉整体结构的找形与预测提供了新思路。

Abstract: Tensegrity form-finding and physical property prediction are fundamental inverse problems in structural mechanics, which aim to determine equilibrium configurations and internal force distributions. These problems are challenging due to strong nonlinearity arising from the coupling between geometry and forces, the need to ensure structural stability, and the enforcement of constraints such as boundary conditions and symmetry. Moreover, traditional methods often lack robustness to noise and outliers. This paper proposes an energy-based learning framework for clustered tensegrity form finding and physical property prediction. The proposed approach incorporates total potential energy minimization and constitutive relations into the training objective, enabling the simultaneous prediction of equilibrium nodal configurations and associated physical quantities, including member forces and force densities. By incorporating energy-based physical losses directly into the learning process, the framework improves physical consistency, robustness, and data efficiency. Numerical experiments on tensegrity structures, including prism and lander systems, show the great potential of the proposed approach and demonstrate its capability for scalable form finding and accurate prediction of structural properties.

### [238] [Contrastive-Collapsed Loss for Flexible and Geometrically Optimal Embeddings and Faster Convergence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12916)
*Blanca Cano-Camarero,Ángela Fernández-Pascual,José R. Dorronsoro*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的损失函数（如交叉熵、点回归）在学习规范化且结构良好的表征时存在不足，如初始化离最优配置较远、梯度信息不够丰富、类间坍塌激励不足等问题。作者希望设计一种既能促进类内坍塌（intra-class collapse）又能实现类间对比（inter-class contrast）的损失函数，同时保留神经网络逼近几何最优嵌入的灵活性。

Method: 提出CoCo损失函数，其核心思想是同时鼓励类内表征聚合和类间表征分离（大角度分离）。通过理论分析将CoCo与点回归、交叉熵等目标函数进行对比，证明CoCo具有更接近最优配置的初始化、信息量更丰富的梯度以及更强的类表征坍塌激励。在OpenML-CC18基准的多个表格数据集上进行实验验证。

Result: 在多样化的表格数据集上，CoCo取得了与核SVM、随机森林、点回归和基于交叉熵的神经网络等SOTA方法相竞争的性能。理论和实验均表明CoCo促进了更紧致的类聚类和更快的收敛速度。

Conclusion: CoCo损失函数是一种有效的目标函数，能够在保持竞争性预测性能的同时学习具有判别力的表征，兼具理论上的优越性和实践中的高效性。

Abstract: In this work, we introduce CoCo, a loss function aimed at learning normalized and well-structured representations. The proposed loss encourages intra-class collapse and inter-class contrast while preserving sufficient flexibility for neural networks to approximate geometrically optimal embeddings with large angular separation between classes. We provide a theoretical analysis positioning CoCo with respect to related objectives such as dot regression and cross-entropy, showing that the new proposed loss benefits from closer initialization to the optimal configuration, more informative gradients, and stronger incentives for class-wise representation collapse. Extensive experiments on diverse tabular datasets from the OpenML-CC18 benchmark show that CoCo achieves competitive performance with state-of-the-art methods, including kernel SVM, Random Forest, dot regression, and cross-entropy-based neural networks. In addition, both theoretical arguments and empirical analyses demonstrate that the proposal promotes tighter class clustering and faster convergence. These results highlight CoCo loss as an effective objective for learning discriminative representations while maintaining competitive predictive performance.

### [239] [Efficient Sequential Calibration with $O(T^{2/3-ε})$ Error Bound](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12928)
*Zihan Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种高效随机预测方法，将校准误差从经典下界 \(T^{2/3}\) 突破至 \(O(T^{2/3-\varepsilon})\)，通过结合 SPR-Calibration 与 Blackwell 校正层实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 突破在线二元序列校准问题中长期存在的 \(T^{2/3}\) 校准误差障碍，寻求更优的误差上界。

Method: 将 SPR-Calibration 程序（控制代理条件均值序列的校准误差）与外部 Blackwell 风格校正层（控制代理序列与真实结果之间的残差）相结合。

Result: 实现了期望校准误差 \(O(T^{2/3-\varepsilon})\)，其中 \(\varepsilon>0\) 为常数，优于经典 \(T^{2/3}\) 下界。

Conclusion: 通过分解总校准误差为代理校准误差与残差，并用二次势能论证及 SPR-Calibration 的稀疏性控制后者，成功突破了长期存在的误差下界。

Abstract: We study the online binary sequential calibration problem. A recent breakthrough by \citet{dagan2024breaking} overcomes the classical \(T^{2/3}\) barrier for calibration error. Building on this result, we present an efficient randomized forecaster that achieves an expected calibration error \(O(T^{2/3-\varepsilon})\) for some constant \(\varepsilon>0\).
  Our forecaster combines the \textsc{SPR-Calibration} procedure \citep{dagan2024breaking} with an outer Blackwell-style correction layer. The \textsc{SPR-Calibration} procedure controls calibration with respect to a surrogate sequence of conditional-mean estimates, while the correction layer controls the additional error incurred when these surrogates are used to approximate the true outcomes. The analysis decomposes the total calibration error into the surrogate calibration error and the residual discrepancy between the surrogate sequence and the true outcomes. The former is bounded by the \textsc{SPR-Calibration} guarantee in \citet{dagan2024breaking}, and the latter is controlled using a quadratic potential argument together with the sparsity of the \textsc{SPR-Calibration} forecaster.

</details>


### [240] [The Spectrum Is Not Enough: When Context Helps Time-Series Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13006)
*Mert Onur Cakiroglu,Mehmet Dalkilic,Hasan Kurban*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文指出，现有的频谱可预测性指标无法回答“加入上下文是否有助于预测”这一实际问题。作者证明，频谱指标对相位随机化不变，而检索型或基础模型提供的超二阶价值则不然。通过替代对实验和覆盖率亏缺诊断，作者验证了超频谱结构才是决定上下文价值的真正因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有频谱可预测性指标被广泛用于判断是否应加入上下文（如更长回看、检索插件、预训练模型），但这两个问题本质不同。频谱指标衡量的是序列自身的可预测性，而上下文的价值取决于操作点（operating point），而非序列本身。作者希望厘清这一混淆，并提供更好的诊断工具。

Method: 作者提出不可能性结果：任何基于功率谱的指标对相位随机化不变，而检索和基础模型的超二阶价值会因相位随机化而崩溃（因为相位随机化后序列渐近高斯）。构造替代对（surrogate pairs）固定频谱和边缘分布；提出覆盖率亏缺（coverage deficit）诊断，其主项衡量超频谱结构（模拟预测相对于线性预测的增益）。在7个基准上验证。

Result: 基于窗口的检索价值在替代对中崩溃（ECL中位数从+33%降至-35%，p<10^{-40}），而所有频谱指标保持不变；基础模型的价值分裂为幸存二阶部分和崩溃的超线性部分；更长的线性窗口的价值幸存。留一数据集验证中，结构项能预测超频谱价值的符号，而频谱指标则相反。

Conclusion: 频谱可预测性指标不能作为判断上下文价值的依据。作者提出的覆盖率亏缺诊断能更好地预测部署决策。本文不引入新预测器，贡献在于概念区分、受控对比和实际诊断工具。

Abstract: A growing family of indices scores how predictable a series is from its spectrum. Practitioners increasingly read these scores as answering a different question: whether \emph{adding context}, a longer lookback, a retrieval plug-in, or a pretrained model, will help. These are not the same question. The value of context is a property of the operating point, not of the series. Any index built from the power spectrum is invariant under phase randomization, whereas the beyond-second-order value that retrieval and foundation models supply is not, because a phase-randomized series is asymptotically Gaussian. We state this as an impossibility result and isolate it with surrogate pairs that fix the spectrum and the marginal by construction. We then give a label-free, configuration-level diagnostic, the coverage deficit, whose principal term measures beyond-spectrum structure as the gain of analog over linear prediction. On seven benchmarks the prediction holds: window-keyed retrieval's value collapses across surrogate pairs (ECL median $+33\%\!\to\!-35\%$, $p{<}10^{-40}$) while every spectral index stays frozen; a foundation model's value splits into a surviving second-order part and a small beyond-linear margin that collapses; a longer linear window's value survives. Leave-one-dataset-out, the structure term predicts the sign of beyond-spectrum value where the spectral indices trail it, and the reverse holds for the second-order mechanism. We introduce no new forecaster; the contribution is the distinction, a controlled comparison, and a diagnostic for the deployment decision. Code: https://anonymous.4open.science/r/SINE.

</details>


### [241] [TerraZero: Procedural Driving Simulation for Zero-Demonstration Self-Play at Scale](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13028)
*Zhouchonghao Wu,Akshay Rangesh,Weixin Li,Wei-Jer Chang,Zachary Lee,Tim Wang,Wei Zhan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: TerraZero 是一个高速过程式驾驶模拟器与自博弈训练框架，在单个服务器级 GPU 上每秒可运行 130 万智能体步数，仅使用随机化地图与规则型交通参与者，从头通过强化学习训练得到零样本泛化的驾驶策略，在 InterPlan 长尾基准和 Waymo Open Sim Agents 上均取得了领先性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有驾驶模拟器难以同时满足三个需求：足够快以支撑大规模强化学习、足够真实以反映真实地图结构、足够多样以覆盖长尾安全关键场景，而日志数据中几乎不包含这类罕见场景。

Method: 1）C 引擎在 CPU 运行模拟、GPU 运行策略推理，通过零拷贝路径实现高速；2）只从日志数据提取地图几何，其余全部随机化（路网、交通信号、智能体动力学/奖励/大小）；3）纯强化学习自博弈训练，无人类演示、无后备规划器。

Result: 1.3M 智能体步/秒（单 GPU）；零样本跨城市/数据集泛化（含无监督左舵驾驶）；InterPlan 长尾基准第一；val14 日常驾驶基准中碰撞率与碰撞时间最佳；Waymo Open Sim Agents 上优于其他无演示方法。

Conclusion: TerraZero 证明了纯强化学习自博弈训练的驾驶策略可以超越依赖人类演示或规划器的大模型方法，且同一框架既能训练驾驶策略，又能训练仿真智能体（同时控制车辆、行人、自行车）。

Abstract: Training robust autonomous driving agents requires a simulator that is fast enough for reinforcement learning at scale, realistic enough to ground behavior in real-world map structure, and diverse enough to cover the safety-critical long tail that logged data rarely contains. We present TerraZero, a procedural driving simulator and self-play training stack. A configurable C engine runs simulation on the CPU and policy inference on the GPU over a zero-copy path, sustaining 1.3M agent-steps per second on a single server-grade GPU, far faster than existing object-level simulators, while keeping fidelity lighter single-agent systems omit: heterogeneous agents, multiple dynamics models, and full traffic-rule enforcement. TerraZero treats logged data only as a source of real-world map geometry, populating each map with randomized rule-based road users and signal controllers and randomizing agent dynamics, rewards, and sizes per episode, so a map yields an unbounded set of scenarios. Every reported policy trains from scratch by reinforcement learning alone on a compute-efficient self-play recipe across GPUs, with zero human demonstrations and no fallback planner at inference. Policies generalize zero-shot across cities and datasets, including emergent left-hand-traffic driving without explicit supervision. As an ego policy, TerraZero is the first fully learned policy to top the InterPlan long-tail benchmark, ahead of larger learned planners; on routine-driving val14 it ranks among the best approaches and is the safest, posting the best collision and time-to-collision scores. On Waymo Open Sim Agents realism the same recipe outperforms other demonstration-free methods and is competitive with the strongest reference-anchored self-play method. One stack serves both roles: driving policies across dynamics for cars and trucks, and sim agents that jointly control vehicles, pedestrians, and cyclists.

### [242] [The Seriality Gap in Video Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13031)
*Jorge Diaz Chao,Konpat Preechakul,Yuxi Liu,Yutong Bai*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 视频扩散模型在多球硬球动力学任务中，当因果链变长时性能下降，而单球控制实验表明这源于依赖事件结构而非视频长度。研究发现存在"序列性差距"：任务需要可扩展的串行计算，但扩散模型的去噪循环无法提供这种能力。理论证明去噪步数不能增加超出骨干网络的串行计算量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究视频扩散模型在处理需要串行推理的物理模拟任务（如多球碰撞）时的局限性，特别是因果链长度对模型性能的影响。

Method: 通过多球硬球动力学实验对比标准双向视频扩散与单球控制实验，进行干预研究（自回归/分块生成、增加网络深度），并从理论上证明去噪步数无法增加串行计算量。

Result: 标准双向视频扩散在多球碰撞任务中随因果链增长性能下降；单球控制中退化消失；增加串行计算的方法（自回归、更深网络）显著提升性能；理论证明去噪步数不增加串行计算。

Conclusion: 揭示了视频扩散模型在串行推理任务上的根本性局限——"序列性差距"，为改进视频预测模型在物理模拟和因果推理任务上的设计提供了理论指导。

Abstract: When one ball strikes another, then another, video models should predict the consequences of each bounce. In controlled experiments on multi-ball hard-sphere dynamics, we find that the performance of standard bidirectional video diffusion degrades as the causal chain lengthens, even when provided more denoising steps. In a length-matched single-ball control, where ball-ball interactions are absent, the degradation largely disappears, isolating dependent-event structure rather than video length as the cause. Across intervention studies, methods that increase effective serial computation improve performance disproportionately, including autoregressive/blockwise generation and architectural depth. We identify this pattern as the seriality gap: a mismatch between tasks requiring growing serial computation and video diffusion models whose denoising loop does not provide scalable serial compute. We then prove that, for deterministic video prediction, denoising steps do not add serial computation beyond the backbone, indicating a structural obstacle for video diffusion on serial reasoning and simulation tasks.

</details>
